    variable PLP_DWT_HAAR_f32

    const plp_dwt_wavelet_f32 PLP_DWT_HAAR_f32 = {
    .length = 2,
    .type = PLP_DWT_WAVELET_HAAR,
    .dec_lo = (float32_t []){
    0.707106781186547570f,   0.707106781186547570f
    },
    .dec_hi = (float32_t []){
   -0.707106781186547570f,   0.707106781186547570f
    }
};
